  "content": "/*\n * Licensed to the Apache Software Foundation (ASF) under one or more\n * contributor license agreements. See the NOTICE file distributed with\n * this work for additional information regarding copyright ownership.\n * The ASF licenses this file to You under the Apache License, Version 2.0\n * (the \"License\"); you may not use this file except in compliance with\n * the License. You may obtain a copy of the License at\n *\n *    http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0\n *\n * Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software\n * distributed under the License is distributed on an \"AS IS\" BASIS,\n * WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.\n * See the License for the specific language governing permissions and\n * limitations under the License.\n */\npackage org.apache.kafka.common.record.internal;\n\nimport org.apache.kafka.common.InvalidRecordException;\nimport org.apache.kafka.common.KafkaException;\nimport org.apache.kafka.common.compress.Compression;\nimport org.apache.kafka.common.errors.CorruptRecordException;\nimport org.apache.kafka.common.header.Header;\nimport org.apache.kafka.common.record.TimestampType;\nimport org.apache.kafka.common.utils.BufferSupplier;\nimport org.apache.kafka.common.utils.ByteBufferOutputStream;\nimport org.apache.kafka.common.utils.ByteUtils;\nimport org.apache.kafka.common.utils.CloseableIterator;\nimport org.apache.kafka.common.utils.Crc32C;\n\nimport java.io.IOException;\nimport java.io.InputStream;\nimport java.nio.BufferUnderflowException;\nimport java.nio.ByteBuffer;\nimport java.util.ArrayList;\nimport java.util.Collections;\nimport java.util.Iterator;\nimport java.util.List;\nimport java.util.NoSuchElementException;\nimport java.util.Objects;\nimport java.util.OptionalLong;\n\nimport static org.apache.kafka.common.record.internal.Records.LOG_OVERHEAD;\n\n/**\n * {@link RecordBatch} implementation for magic v2 and above. This class provides both read and\n * in-place-mutation access to a single batch encoded in the Kafka binary wire format. The on-wire\n * schema is:\n *\n * <pre>\n * RecordBatch =&gt;\n *   BaseOffset            =&gt; Int64\n *   Length                =&gt; Int32\n *   PartitionLeaderEpoch  =&gt; Int32\n *   Magic                 =&gt; Int8\n *   CRC                   =&gt; Uint32\n *   Attributes            =&gt; Int16\n *   LastOffsetDelta       =&gt; Int32  // also serves as LastSequenceDelta\n *   BaseTimestamp         =&gt; Int64\n *   MaxTimestamp          =&gt; Int64\n *   ProducerId            =&gt; Int64\n *   ProducerEpoch         =&gt; Int16\n *   BaseSequence          =&gt; Int32\n *   RecordsCount          =&gt; Int32\n *   Records               =&gt; [Record]\n * </pre>\n *\n * <p>When compression is enabled (see attributes below), the compressed record data is serialized\n * directly following the count of the number of records.\n *\n * <p>The CRC covers the data from the attributes to the end of the batch (i.e. all the bytes that\n * follow the CRC). It is located after the magic byte, which means that clients must parse the\n * magic byte before deciding how to interpret the bytes between the batch length and the magic\n * byte. The partition leader epoch field is not included in the CRC computation to avoid the need\n * to recompute the CRC when this field is assigned for every batch that is received by the broker.\n * The CRC-32C (Castagnoli) polynomial is used for the computation.\n *\n * <p><b>Compaction:</b> Unlike the older message formats, magic v2 and above preserves the first\n * and last offset/sequence numbers from the original batch when the log is cleaned. This is\n * required in order to be able to restore the producer's state when the log is reloaded. If we did\n * not retain the last sequence number, then following a partition leader failure, once the new\n * leader has rebuilt the producer state from the log, the next sequence expected number would no\n * longer be in sync with what was written by the client. This would cause an unexpected\n * {@code OutOfOrderSequence} error, which is typically fatal. The base sequence number must be\n * preserved for duplicate checking: the broker checks incoming Produce requests for duplicates by\n * verifying that the first and last sequence numbers of the incoming batch match the last from that\n * producer.\n *\n * <p>Note that if all of the records in a batch are removed during compaction, the broker may\n * still retain an empty batch header in order to preserve the producer sequence information as\n * described above. These empty batches are retained only until either a new sequence number is\n * written by the corresponding producer or the producerId is expired from lack of activity.\n *\n * <p>There is no similar need to preserve the timestamp from the original batch after compaction.\n * The {@code BaseTimestamp} field therefore reflects the timestamp of the first record in the\n * batch in most cases. If the batch is empty, the {@code BaseTimestamp} will be set to\n * {@link RecordBatch#NO_TIMESTAMP}. If the delete horizon flag is set to 1, the\n * {@code BaseTimestamp} will be set to the time at which tombstone records and aborted transaction\n * markers in the batch should be removed.\n *\n * <p>Similarly, the {@code MaxTimestamp} field reflects the maximum timestamp of the current\n * records if the timestamp type is {@link TimestampType#CREATE_TIME}. For\n * {@link TimestampType#LOG_APPEND_TIME}, on the other hand, the {@code MaxTimestamp} field\n * reflects the timestamp set by the broker and is preserved after compaction. Additionally, the\n * {@code MaxTimestamp} of an empty batch always retains the previous value prior to becoming empty.\n *\n * <p>The current attributes bit layout:\n * <pre>\n *  ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n *  | Unused (7-15) | Delete Horizon Flag (6) | Control (5) | Transactional (4) | Timestamp Type (3) | Compression Type (0-2) |\n *  ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * </pre>\n *\n * <p><b>Thread-safety:</b> This class is <em>not</em> thread-safe. The underlying\n * {@link ByteBuffer} is accessed without synchronisation. Concurrent reads or any combination of\n * reads and in-place mutations (e.g. {@link #setLastOffset}, {@link #setMaxTimestamp},\n * {@link #setPartitionLeaderEpoch}) from multiple threads requires external synchronisation.\n *\n * @see RecordBatch\n * @see MemoryRecords\n * @see MemoryRecordsBuilder\n */\npublic class DefaultRecordBatch extends AbstractRecordBatch implements MutableRecordBatch {\n    static final int BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET = 0;\n    static final int BASE_OFFSET_LENGTH = 8;\n    static final int LENGTH_OFFSET = BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET + BASE_OFFSET_LENGTH;\n    static final int LENGTH_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET = LENGTH_OFFSET + LENGTH_LENGTH;\n    static final int PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int MAGIC_OFFSET = PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET + PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_LENGTH;\n    static final int MAGIC_LENGTH = 1;\n    public static final int CRC_OFFSET = MAGIC_OFFSET + MAGIC_LENGTH;\n    static final int CRC_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET = CRC_OFFSET + CRC_LENGTH;\n    static final int ATTRIBUTE_LENGTH = 2;\n    public static final int LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_OFFSET = ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET + ATTRIBUTE_LENGTH;\n    static final int LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int BASE_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET = LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_OFFSET + LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_LENGTH;\n    static final int BASE_TIMESTAMP_LENGTH = 8;\n    static final int MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET = BASE_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET + BASE_TIMESTAMP_LENGTH;\n    static final int MAX_TIMESTAMP_LENGTH = 8;\n    static final int PRODUCER_ID_OFFSET = MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET + MAX_TIMESTAMP_LENGTH;\n    static final int PRODUCER_ID_LENGTH = 8;\n    static final int PRODUCER_EPOCH_OFFSET = PRODUCER_ID_OFFSET + PRODUCER_ID_LENGTH;\n    static final int PRODUCER_EPOCH_LENGTH = 2;\n    static final int BASE_SEQUENCE_OFFSET = PRODUCER_EPOCH_OFFSET + PRODUCER_EPOCH_LENGTH;\n    static final int BASE_SEQUENCE_LENGTH = 4;\n    public static final int RECORDS_COUNT_OFFSET = BASE_SEQUENCE_OFFSET + BASE_SEQUENCE_LENGTH;\n    static final int RECORDS_COUNT_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int RECORDS_OFFSET = RECORDS_COUNT_OFFSET + RECORDS_COUNT_LENGTH;\n    public static final int RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD = RECORDS_OFFSET;\n\n    private static final byte COMPRESSION_CODEC_MASK = 0x07;\n    private static final byte TRANSACTIONAL_FLAG_MASK = 0x10;\n    private static final int CONTROL_FLAG_MASK = 0x20;\n    private static final byte DELETE_HORIZON_FLAG_MASK = 0x40;\n    private static final byte TIMESTAMP_TYPE_MASK = 0x08;\n\n    private final ByteBuffer buffer;\n\n    DefaultRecordBatch(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n        this.buffer = buffer;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public byte magic() {\n        return buffer.get(MAGIC_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void ensureValid() {\n        if (sizeInBytes() < RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD)\n            throw new CorruptRecordException(\"Record batch is corrupt (the size \" + sizeInBytes() +\n                    \" is smaller than the minimum allowed overhead \" + RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD + \")\");\n\n        if (!isValid())\n            throw new CorruptRecordException(\"Record is corrupt (stored crc = \" + checksum()\n                    + \", computed crc = \" + computeChecksum() + \")\");\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Gets the base timestamp of the batch, which is used to calculate each individual record's\n     * absolute timestamp from its delta value encoded in the record.\n     *\n     * <p>For batches where the delete horizon flag is set, the base timestamp field is overloaded\n     * to store the delete horizon instead. Use {@link #deleteHorizonMs()} to access that value\n     * safely.\n     *\n     * @return The base timestamp in milliseconds since the Unix epoch\n     * @see #deleteHorizonMs()\n     */\n    public long baseTimestamp() {\n        return buffer.getLong(BASE_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long maxTimestamp() {\n        return buffer.getLong(MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public TimestampType timestampType() {\n        return (attributes() & TIMESTAMP_TYPE_MASK) == 0 ? TimestampType.CREATE_TIME : TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long baseOffset() {\n        return buffer.getLong(BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long lastOffset() {\n        return baseOffset() + lastOffsetDelta();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long producerId() {\n        return buffer.getLong(PRODUCER_ID_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public short producerEpoch() {\n        return buffer.getShort(PRODUCER_EPOCH_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int baseSequence() {\n        return buffer.getInt(BASE_SEQUENCE_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    private int lastOffsetDelta() {\n        return buffer.getInt(LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int lastSequence() {\n        int baseSequence = baseSequence();\n        if (baseSequence == RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE)\n            return RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE;\n        return incrementSequence(baseSequence, lastOffsetDelta());\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public CompressionType compressionType() {\n        return CompressionType.forId(attributes() & COMPRESSION_CODEC_MASK);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int sizeInBytes() {\n        return LOG_OVERHEAD + buffer.getInt(LENGTH_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    private int count() {\n        return buffer.getInt(RECORDS_COUNT_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Integer countOrNull() {\n        return count();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void writeTo(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n        buffer.put(this.buffer.duplicate());\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void writeTo(ByteBufferOutputStream outputStream) {\n        outputStream.write(this.buffer.duplicate());\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean isTransactional() {\n        return (attributes() & TRANSACTIONAL_FLAG_MASK) > 0;\n    }\n\n    private boolean hasDeleteHorizonMs() {\n        return (attributes() & DELETE_HORIZON_FLAG_MASK) > 0;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public OptionalLong deleteHorizonMs() {\n        if (hasDeleteHorizonMs())\n            return OptionalLong.of(buffer.getLong(BASE_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET));\n        else\n            return OptionalLong.empty();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean isControlBatch() {\n        return (attributes() & CONTROL_FLAG_MASK) > 0;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int partitionLeaderEpoch() {\n        return buffer.getInt(PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Returns an {@link InputStream} that reads the raw (possibly compressed) record bytes of this\n     * batch, starting immediately after the fixed batch header.\n     *\n     * <p>If compression is enabled, the stream transparently wraps the underlying buffer bytes\n     * with the appropriate decompression codec, using buffers obtained from the supplied\n     * {@link BufferSupplier} to reduce allocations.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Performance note:</b> The returned stream may hold a buffer obtained from\n     * {@code bufferSupplier}. Callers must close the stream after use to release that buffer back\n     * to the supplier pool.\n     *\n     * @param bufferSupplier supplier of temporary decompression buffers; must not be {@code null}\n     * @return an {@link InputStream} over the (possibly decompressed) record bytes\n     */\n    public InputStream recordInputStream(BufferSupplier bufferSupplier) {\n        final ByteBuffer buffer = this.buffer.duplicate();\n        buffer.position(RECORDS_OFFSET);\n        return Compression.of(compressionType()).build().wrapForInput(buffer, magic(), bufferSupplier);\n    }\n\n    private CloseableIterator<Record> compressedIterator(BufferSupplier bufferSupplier, boolean skipKeyValue) {\n        final InputStream inputStream = recordInputStream(bufferSupplier);\n\n        if (skipKeyValue) {\n            return new StreamRecordIterator(inputStream) {\n                @Override\n                protected Record doReadRecord(long baseOffset, long baseTimestamp, int baseSequence, Long logAppendTime) throws IOException {\n                    return DefaultRecord.readPartiallyFrom(inputStream, baseOffset, baseTimestamp, baseSequence, logAppendTime);\n                }\n            };\n        } else {\n            return new StreamRecordIterator(inputStream) {\n                @Override\n                protected Record doReadRecord(long baseOffset, long baseTimestamp, int baseSequence, Long logAppendTime) throws IOException {\n                    return DefaultRecord.readFrom(inputStream, baseOffset, baseTimestamp, baseSequence, logAppendTime);\n                }\n            };\n        }\n    }\n\n    private CloseableIterator<Record> uncompressedIterator() {\n        final ByteBuffer buffer = this.buffer.duplicate();\n        buffer.position(RECORDS_OFFSET);\n        return new RecordIterator() {\n            @Override\n            protected Record readNext(long baseOffset, long baseTimestamp, int baseSequence, Long logAppendTime) {\n                try {\n                    return DefaultRecord.readFrom(buffer, baseOffset, baseTimestamp, baseSequence, logAppendTime);\n                } catch (BufferUnderflowException e) {\n                    throw new InvalidRecordException(\"Incorrect declared batch size, premature EOF reached\");\n                }\n            }\n            @Override\n            protected boolean ensureNoneRemaining() {\n                return !buffer.hasRemaining();\n            }\n            @Override\n            public void close() {}\n        };\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Iterator<Record> iterator() {\n        if (count() == 0)\n            return Collections.emptyIterator();\n\n        if (!isCompressed())\n            return uncompressedIterator();\n\n        // for a normal iterator, we cannot ensure that the underlying compression stream is closed,\n        // so we decompress the full record set here. Use cases which call for a lower memory footprint\n        // can use `streamingIterator` at the cost of additional complexity\n        try (CloseableIterator<Record> iterator = compressedIterator(BufferSupplier.NO_CACHING, false)) {\n            List<Record> records = new ArrayList<>(count());\n            while (iterator.hasNext())\n                records.add(iterator.next());\n            return records.iterator();\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public CloseableIterator<Record> skipKeyValueIterator(BufferSupplier bufferSupplier) {\n        if (count() == 0) {\n            return CloseableIterator.wrap(Collections.emptyIterator());\n        }\n\n        /*\n         * For uncompressed iterator, it is actually not worth skipping key / value / headers at all since\n         * its ByteBufferInputStream's skip() function is less efficient compared with just reading it actually\n         * as it will allocate new byte array.\n         */\n        if (!isCompressed())\n            return uncompressedIterator();\n\n        // we define this to be a closable iterator so that caller (i.e. the log validator) needs to close it\n        // while we can save memory footprint of not decompressing the full record set ahead of time\n        return compressedIterator(bufferSupplier, true);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public CloseableIterator<Record> streamingIterator(BufferSupplier bufferSupplier) {\n        if (isCompressed())\n            return compressedIterator(bufferSupplier, false);\n        else\n            return uncompressedIterator();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void setLastOffset(long offset) {\n        buffer.putLong(BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET, offset - lastOffsetDelta());\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void setMaxTimestamp(TimestampType timestampType, long maxTimestamp) {\n        long currentMaxTimestamp = maxTimestamp();\n        // We don't need to recompute crc if the timestamp is not updated.\n        if (timestampType() == timestampType && currentMaxTimestamp == maxTimestamp)\n            return;\n\n        byte attributes = computeAttributes(compressionType(), timestampType, isTransactional(), isControlBatch(), hasDeleteHorizonMs());\n        buffer.putShort(ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET, attributes);\n        buffer.putLong(MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET, maxTimestamp);\n        long crc = computeChecksum();\n        ByteUtils.writeUnsignedInt(buffer, CRC_OFFSET, crc);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void setPartitionLeaderEpoch(int epoch) {\n        buffer.putInt(PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET, epoch);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long checksum() {\n        return ByteUtils.readUnsignedInt(buffer, CRC_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    public boolean isValid() {\n        return sizeInBytes() >= RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD && checksum() == computeChecksum();\n    }\n\n    private long computeChecksum() {\n        return Crc32C.compute(buffer, ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET, buffer.limit() - ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    private byte attributes() {\n        // note we're not using the second byte of attributes\n        return (byte) buffer.getShort(ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean equals(Object o) {\n        if (this == o)\n            return true;\n        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass())\n            return false;\n\n        DefaultRecordBatch that = (DefaultRecordBatch) o;\n        return Objects.equals(buffer, that.buffer);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int hashCode() {\n        return buffer != null ? buffer.hashCode() : 0;\n    }\n\n    private static byte computeAttributes(CompressionType type, TimestampType timestampType,\n                                          boolean isTransactional, boolean isControl, boolean isDeleteHorizonSet) {\n        if (timestampType == TimestampType.NO_TIMESTAMP_TYPE)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Timestamp type must be provided to compute attributes for message \" +\n                    \"format v2 and above\");\n\n        byte attributes = isTransactional ? TRANSACTIONAL_FLAG_MASK : 0;\n        if (isControl)\n            attributes |= CONTROL_FLAG_MASK;\n        if (type.id > 0)\n            attributes |= (byte) (COMPRESSION_CODEC_MASK & type.id);\n        if (timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME)\n            attributes |= TIMESTAMP_TYPE_MASK;\n        if (isDeleteHorizonSet)\n            attributes |= DELETE_HORIZON_FLAG_MASK;\n        return attributes;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Writes an empty (zero-record) batch header into the given buffer at its current position.\n     * This is used during log compaction to preserve producer sequence metadata when all records\n     * in a batch have been deleted.\n     *\n     * <p>The written header occupies exactly {@link #RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD} bytes. The CRC is\n     * computed and written as part of this call.\n     *\n     * @param buffer               the destination buffer; must have at least\n     *                             {@link #RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD} bytes remaining\n     * @param magic                the record format magic byte; must be\n     *                             {@link RecordBatch#MAGIC_VALUE_V2} or higher\n     * @param producerId           the producer id to embed in the header\n     * @param producerEpoch        the producer epoch to embed in the header\n     * @param baseSequence         the base sequence number to embed in the header\n     * @param baseOffset           the base (first) offset of the original batch\n     * @param lastOffset           the last offset of the original batch\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch the leader epoch at the time the batch was written\n     * @param timestampType        the timestamp type ({@link TimestampType#CREATE_TIME} or\n     *                             {@link TimestampType#LOG_APPEND_TIME})\n     * @param timestamp            the timestamp to record in the header\n     * @param isTransactional      whether this batch was produced as part of a transaction\n     * @param isControlRecord      whether this batch is a control batch\n     * @see #writeHeader\n     */\n    public static void writeEmptyHeader(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                        byte magic,\n                                        long producerId,\n                                        short producerEpoch,\n                                        int baseSequence,\n                                        long baseOffset,\n                                        long lastOffset,\n                                        int partitionLeaderEpoch,\n                                        TimestampType timestampType,\n                                        long timestamp,\n                                        boolean isTransactional,\n                                        boolean isControlRecord) {\n        int offsetDelta = (int) (lastOffset - baseOffset);\n        writeHeader(buffer, baseOffset, offsetDelta, DefaultRecordBatch.RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD, magic,\n                    CompressionType.NONE, timestampType, RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP, timestamp, producerId,\n                    producerEpoch, baseSequence, isTransactional, isControlRecord, false, partitionLeaderEpoch, 0);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Encodes a complete magic v2 batch header into the given buffer at its current position and\n     * advances the buffer position by {@link #RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD} bytes. The CRC-32C checksum\n     * covering all header fields from the attributes to the end of the declared batch size is\n     * computed and written inline.\n     *\n     * <p>This is a low-level method used by {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} during batch\n     * serialisation. Most callers should use {@link MemoryRecords#builder} or\n     * {@link #writeEmptyHeader} instead.\n     *\n     * @param buffer               the destination buffer; must have at least {@code sizeInBytes}\n     *                             bytes remaining from the current position\n     * @param baseOffset           the base (first) offset of the batch\n     * @param lastOffsetDelta      difference between the last and base offsets in the batch\n     * @param sizeInBytes          total serialised size of the batch in bytes, including this header\n     * @param magic                the record format magic byte; must be\n     *                             {@link RecordBatch#MAGIC_VALUE_V2} or higher\n     * @param compressionType      the compression codec used for the record data\n     * @param timestampType        the timestamp type ({@link TimestampType#CREATE_TIME} or\n     *                             {@link TimestampType#LOG_APPEND_TIME})\n     * @param baseTimestamp        the base timestamp; used to compute per-record timestamp deltas,\n     *                             or {@link RecordBatch#NO_TIMESTAMP} if not applicable\n     * @param maxTimestamp         the maximum timestamp among all records in the batch\n     * @param producerId           the idempotent/transactional producer id, or\n     *                             {@link RecordBatch#NO_PRODUCER_ID}\n     * @param epoch                the producer epoch, or {@link RecordBatch#NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH}\n     * @param sequence             the base sequence number, or {@link RecordBatch#NO_SEQUENCE}\n     * @param isTransactional      whether this batch belongs to a transaction\n     * @param isControlBatch       whether this is a control batch\n     * @param isDeleteHorizonSet   whether the delete horizon flag should be set in the attributes;\n     *                             when true, {@code baseTimestamp} encodes the delete horizon time\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch the leader epoch at the time of writing\n     * @param numRecords           number of records contained in the batch\n     * @throws IllegalArgumentException if {@code magic} is below\n     *         {@link RecordBatch#CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE} or if {@code baseTimestamp} is negative and\n     *         not equal to {@link RecordBatch#NO_TIMESTAMP}\n     */\n    public static void writeHeader(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                   long baseOffset,\n                                   int lastOffsetDelta,\n                                   int sizeInBytes,\n                                   byte magic,\n                                   CompressionType compressionType,\n                                   TimestampType timestampType,\n                                   long baseTimestamp,\n                                   long maxTimestamp,\n                                   long producerId,\n                                   short epoch,\n                                   int sequence,\n                                   boolean isTransactional,\n                                   boolean isControlBatch,\n                                   boolean isDeleteHorizonSet,\n                                   int partitionLeaderEpoch,\n                                   int numRecords) {\n        if (magic < RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid magic value \" + magic);\n        if (baseTimestamp < 0 && baseTimestamp != NO_TIMESTAMP)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid message timestamp \" + baseTimestamp);\n\n        short attributes = computeAttributes(compressionType, timestampType, isTransactional, isControlBatch, isDeleteHorizonSet);\n\n        int position = buffer.position();\n        buffer.putLong(position + BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET, baseOffset);\n        buffer.putInt(position + LENGTH_OFFSET, sizeInBytes - LOG_OVERHEAD);\n        buffer.putInt(position + PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET, partitionLeaderEpoch);\n        buffer.put(position + MAGIC_OFFSET, magic);\n        buffer.putShort(position + ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET, attributes);\n        buffer.putLong(position + BASE_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET, baseTimestamp);\n        buffer.putLong(position + MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET, maxTimestamp);\n        buffer.putInt(position + LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_OFFSET, lastOffsetDelta);\n        buffer.putLong(position + PRODUCER_ID_OFFSET, producerId);\n        buffer.putShort(position + PRODUCER_EPOCH_OFFSET, epoch);\n        buffer.putInt(position + BASE_SEQUENCE_OFFSET, sequence);\n        buffer.putInt(position + RECORDS_COUNT_OFFSET, numRecords);\n        long crc = Crc32C.compute(buffer, ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET, sizeInBytes - ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET);\n        buffer.putInt(position + CRC_OFFSET, (int) crc);\n        buffer.position(position + RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public String toString() {\n        return \"RecordBatch(magic=\" + magic() + \", offsets=[\" + baseOffset() + \", \" + lastOffset() + \"], \" +\n                \"sequence=[\" + baseSequence() + \", \" + lastSequence() + \"], \" +\n                \"partitionLeaderEpoch=\" + partitionLeaderEpoch() + \", \" +\n                \"isTransactional=\" + isTransactional() + \", isControlBatch=\" + isControlBatch() + \", \" +\n                \"compression=\" + compressionType() + \", timestampType=\" + timestampType() + \", crc=\" + checksum() + \")\";\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Computes the serialised size in bytes of a magic v2 batch containing the given\n     * {@link Record} objects, starting at {@code baseOffset}.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Performance note:</b> This method iterates over all records in order to accumulate\n     * per-record sizes (including variable-length fields and varint-encoded deltas). It does not\n     * account for the overhead of any compression codec.\n     *\n     * @param baseOffset the base offset of the batch; used to compute per-record offset deltas\n     * @param records    the records whose encoded sizes should be summed; must not be {@code null}\n     * @return the total batch size in bytes (header plus all record bytes), or {@code 0} if\n     *         {@code records} is empty\n     */\n    public static int sizeInBytes(long baseOffset, Iterable<Record> records) {\n        Iterator<Record> iterator = records.iterator();\n        if (!iterator.hasNext())\n            return 0;\n\n        int size = RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD;\n        Long baseTimestamp = null;\n        while (iterator.hasNext()) {\n            Record record = iterator.next();\n            int offsetDelta = (int) (record.offset() - baseOffset);\n            if (baseTimestamp == null)\n                baseTimestamp = record.timestamp();\n            long timestampDelta = record.timestamp() - baseTimestamp;\n            size += DefaultRecord.sizeInBytes(offsetDelta, timestampDelta, record.key(), record.value(),\n                    record.headers());\n        }\n        return size;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Computes the serialised size in bytes of a magic v2 batch containing the given\n     * {@link SimpleRecord} objects, assuming sequential offset assignment starting at delta 0.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Performance note:</b> This method iterates over all records in order to accumulate\n     * per-record sizes. It does not account for the overhead of any compression codec.\n     *\n     * @param records the simple records whose encoded sizes should be summed; must not be\n     *                {@code null}\n     * @return the total batch size in bytes (header plus all record bytes), or {@code 0} if\n     *         {@code records} is empty\n     */\n    public static int sizeInBytes(Iterable<SimpleRecord> records) {\n        Iterator<SimpleRecord> iterator = records.iterator();\n        if (!iterator.hasNext())\n            return 0;\n\n        int size = RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD;\n        int offsetDelta = 0;\n        Long baseTimestamp = null;\n        while (iterator.hasNext()) {\n            SimpleRecord record = iterator.next();\n            if (baseTimestamp == null)\n                baseTimestamp = record.timestamp();\n            long timestampDelta = record.timestamp() - baseTimestamp;\n            size += DefaultRecord.sizeInBytes(offsetDelta++, timestampDelta, record.key(), record.value(),\n                    record.headers());\n        }\n        return size;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Get an upper bound on the size of a batch with only a single record using a given key and value. This\n     * is only an estimate because it does not take into account additional overhead from the compression\n     * algorithm used.\n     */\n    static int estimateBatchSizeUpperBound(ByteBuffer key, ByteBuffer value, Header[] headers) {\n        return RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD + DefaultRecord.recordSizeUpperBound(key, value, headers);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Increments a producer sequence number by {@code increment}, wrapping around at\n     * {@link Integer#MAX_VALUE} according to the Kafka sequence-number arithmetic.\n     *\n     * <p>Kafka sequence numbers are unsigned 31-bit integers that wrap around modulo\n     * {@code Integer.MAX_VALUE + 1}. This method implements the wrap-around correctly so that\n     * brokers can detect duplicate and out-of-order produce requests even across sequence-number\n     * rollovers.\n     *\n     * @param sequence  the current base sequence number; must be non-negative\n     * @param increment the value to add; must be non-negative\n     * @return the resulting sequence number after incrementing, with wrap-around applied\n     * @see #decrementSequence(int, int)\n     */\n    public static int incrementSequence(int sequence, int increment) {\n        if (sequence > Integer.MAX_VALUE - increment)\n            return increment - (Integer.MAX_VALUE - sequence) - 1;\n        return sequence + increment;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Decrements a producer sequence number by {@code decrement}, wrapping around at zero\n     * according to the Kafka sequence-number arithmetic.\n     *\n     * <p>This is the inverse of {@link #incrementSequence(int, int)}. The same modulo\n     * {@code Integer.MAX_VALUE + 1} semantics apply.\n     *\n     * @param sequence  the current sequence number; must be non-negative\n     * @param decrement the value to subtract; must be non-negative\n     * @return the resulting sequence number after decrementing, with wrap-around applied\n     * @see #incrementSequence(int, int)\n     */\n    public static int decrementSequence(int sequence, int decrement) {\n        if (sequence < decrement)\n            return Integer.MAX_VALUE - (decrement - sequence) + 1;\n        return sequence - decrement;\n    }\n\n    // visible for testing\n    abstract class RecordIterator implements CloseableIterator<Record> {\n        private final Long logAppendTime;\n        private final long baseOffset;\n        private final long baseTimestamp;\n        private final int baseSequence;\n        private final int numRecords;\n        private int readRecords = 0;\n\n        RecordIterator() {\n            this.logAppendTime = timestampType() == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME ? maxTimestamp() : null;\n            this.baseOffset = baseOffset();\n            this.baseTimestamp = baseTimestamp();\n            this.baseSequence = baseSequence();\n            int numRecords = count();\n            if (numRecords < 0)\n                throw new InvalidRecordException(\"Found invalid record count \" + numRecords + \" in magic v\" +\n                        magic() + \" batch\");\n            this.numRecords = numRecords;\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        public boolean hasNext() {\n            return readRecords < numRecords;\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        public Record next() {\n            if (readRecords >= numRecords)\n                throw new NoSuchElementException();\n\n            readRecords++;\n            Record rec = readNext(baseOffset, baseTimestamp, baseSequence, logAppendTime);\n            if (readRecords == numRecords) {\n                // Validate that the actual size of the batch is equal to declared size\n                // by checking that after reading declared number of items, there no items left\n                // (overflow case, i.e. reading past buffer end is checked elsewhere).\n                if (!ensureNoneRemaining())\n                    throw new InvalidRecordException(\"Incorrect declared batch size, records still remaining in file\");\n            }\n            return rec;\n        }\n\n        protected abstract Record readNext(long baseOffset, long baseTimestamp, int baseSequence, Long logAppendTime);\n\n        protected abstract boolean ensureNoneRemaining();\n\n        @Override\n        public void remove() {\n            throw new UnsupportedOperationException();\n        }\n\n    }\n\n    // visible for This class is used to read or\n * modify in-place an existing, already-encoded buffer of one or more {@link RecordBatch} objects.\n *\n * <p>To <em>produce</em> new record data into a fresh buffer, use {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} or\n * one of the static factory methods on this class (e.g.\n * {@link #builder(ByteBuffer, byte, Compression, TimestampType, long)},\n * {@link #withRecords}, {@link #withTransactionalRecords}, etc.).\n *\n * <p><b>Performance characteristics:</b>\n * <ul>\n *   <li>Batch metadata (offsets, sizes, timestamps) is read directly from the backing\n *       {@link ByteBuffer} without copying \u2014 access to header fields is O(1).</li>\n *   <li>Record-level access requires iterating and, for compressed batches, decompressing the\n *       record stream. Use {@link RecordBatch#streamingIterator(BufferSupplier)} with a buffer\n *       pool to minimise allocation pressure during decompression.</li>\n *   <li>{@link #validBytes()} is computed lazily on the first call and then cached; subsequent\n *       calls are O(1).</li>\n *   <li>{@link #buffer()} returns a {@link ByteBuffer#duplicate() duplicate} of the internal\n *       buffer \u2014 the position and limit of the returned view are independent of the internal\n *       buffer, but the underlying byte array is shared (no data copy).</li>\n *   <li>{@link #slice(int, int)} returns a zero-copy view over a sub-range of the backing\n *       buffer.</li>\n * </ul>\n *\n * <p><b>Thread-safety:</b> Instances of this class are <em>not</em> thread-safe. The backing\n * {@link ByteBuffer} is accessed without synchronisation. Additionally, in-place mutations\n * performed via {@link MutableRecordBatch} methods (e.g.\n * {@link MutableRecordBatch#setLastOffset setLastOffset},\n * {@link MutableRecordBatch#setMaxTimestamp setMaxTimestamp}) modify the shared buffer\n * in-place and must not race with concurrent readers. This\n     * may be smaller than what is returned by {@link #sizeInBytes()}.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Performance note:</b> The result is computed lazily on the first call by iterating\n     * over all batches and summing their sizes. The computed value is cached; subsequent calls\n     * return the cached result in O(1).\n     *\n     * @return The number of valid bytes\n     */\n    public int validBytes() {\n        if (validBytes >= 0)\n            return validBytes;\n\n        int bytes = 0;\n        for (RecordBatch batch : batches())\n            bytes += batch.sizeInBytes();\n\n        this.validBytes = bytes;\n        return bytes;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public AbstractIterator<MutableRecordBatch> batchIterator() {\n        return new RecordBatchIterator<>(new ByteBufferLogInputStream(buffer.duplicate(), Integer.MAX_VALUE));\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Validates the header of the first batch and returns batch size.\n     *\n     * @return first batch size including LOG_OVERHEAD if buffer contains header up to\n     *         magic byte, null otherwise\n     * @throws CorruptRecordException if record size or magic is invalid\n     */\n    public Integer firstBatchSize() {\n        if (buffer.remaining() < HEADER_SIZE_UP_TO_MAGIC)\n            return null;\n        return new ByteBufferLogInputStream(buffer, Integer.MAX_VALUE).nextBatchSize();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Filter the records into the provided ByteBuffer.\n     *\n     * <p>Each batch is evaluated by the supplied {@link RecordFilter}: the filter first decides\n     * at the batch level (via {@link RecordFilter#checkBatchRetention}) whether the entire batch\n     * can be dropped or must be retained; for batches that pass the batch-level check, individual\n     * records are evaluated via {@link RecordFilter#shouldRetainRecord}. Retained records are\n     * re-serialised into {@code destinationBuffer}, potentially into a new magic v2 batch if the\n     * original batch used an older format or if the delete-horizon flag needs to be set.\n     *\n     * <p>If the destination buffer runs out of space, a larger buffer is allocated automatically\n     * and returned in {@link FilterResult#outputBuffer()}. Callers should always use the buffer\n     * from {@link FilterResult#outputBuffer()} rather than the original {@code destinationBuffer}.\n     *\n     * @param filter                      The filter function\n     * @param destinationBuffer           The byte buffer to write the filtered records to\n     * @param decompressionBufferSupplier The supplier of ByteBuffer(s) used for decompression if supported. For small\n     *                                    record batches, allocating a potentially large buffer (64 KB for LZ4) will\n     *                                    dominate the cost of decompressing and iterating over the records in the\n     *                                    batch. As such, a supplier that reuses buffers will have a significant\n     *                                    performance impact.\n     * @return A FilterResult with a summary of the output (for metrics) and potentially an overflow buffer\n     */\n    public FilterResult filterTo(RecordFilter filter, ByteBuffer destinationBuffer, BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier) {\n        return filterTo(batches(), filter, destinationBuffer, decompressionBufferSupplier);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Note: This method is also used to convert the first timestamp of the batch (which is usually the timestamp of the first record)\n     * to the delete horizon of the tombstones or txn markers which are present in the batch.\n     */\n    private static FilterResult filterTo(Iterable<MutableRecordBatch> batches, RecordFilter filter,\n                                         ByteBuffer destinationBuffer, BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier) {\n        FilterResult filterResult = new FilterResult(destinationBuffer);\n        ByteBufferOutputStream bufferOutputStream = new ByteBufferOutputStream(destinationBuffer);\n        for (MutableRecordBatch batch : batches) {\n            final BatchRetentionResult batchRetentionResult = filter.checkBatchRetention(batch);\n            final boolean containsMarkerForEmptyTxn = batchRetentionResult.containsMarkerForEmptyTxn;\n            final BatchRetention batchRetention = batchRetentionResult.batchRetention;\n\n            filterResult.bytesRead += batch.sizeInBytes();\n\n            if (batchRetention == BatchRetention.DELETE)\n                continue;\n\n            final BatchFilterResult iterationResult = filterBatch(batch, decompressionBufferSupplier, filterResult,\n                filter);\n            List<Record> retainedRecords = iterationResult.retainedRecords;\n            boolean containsTombstones = iterationResult.containsTombstones;\n            boolean writeOriginalBatch = iterationResult.writeOriginalBatch;\n            long maxOffset = iterationResult.maxOffset;\n\n            if (!retainedRecords.isEmpty()) {\n                // we check if the delete horizon should be set to a new value\n                // in which case, we need to reset the base timestamp and overwrite the timestamp deltas\n                // if the batch does not contain tombstones, then we don't need to overwrite batch\n                boolean needToSetDeleteHorizon = (containsTombstones || containsMarkerForEmptyTxn) &&\n                    batch.deleteHorizonMs().isEmpty();\n                if (writeOriginalBatch && !needToSetDeleteHorizon) {\n                    batch.writeTo(bufferOutputStream);\n                    filterResult.updateRetainedBatchMetadata(batch, retainedRecords.size(), false);\n                } else {\n                    long deleteHorizonMs;\n                    if (needToSetDeleteHorizon)\n                        deleteHorizonMs = filter.currentTime + filter.deleteRetentionMs;\n                    else\n                        deleteHorizonMs = batch.deleteHorizonMs().orElse(RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP);\n                    try (final MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = buildRetainedRecordsInto(batch, retainedRecords,\n                            bufferOutputStream, deleteHorizonMs)) {\n                        MemoryRecords records = builder.build();\n                        int filteredBatchSize = records.sizeInBytes();\n                        MemoryRecordsBuilder.RecordsInfo info = builder.info();\n                        filterResult.updateRetainedBatchMetadata(info.maxTimestamp, info.shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp,\n                            maxOffset, retainedRecords.size(), filteredBatchSize);\n                    }\n                }\n            } else if (batchRetention == BatchRetention.RETAIN_EMPTY) {\n                if (batch.magic() < RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2) // should never happen\n                    throw new IllegalStateException(\"Empty batches are only supported for magic v2 and above\");\n\n                bufferOutputStream.ensureRemaining(DefaultRecordBatch.RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD);\n                DefaultRecordBatch.writeEmptyHeader(bufferOutputStream.buffer(), RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, batch.producerId(),\n                        batch.producerEpoch(), batch.baseSequence(), batch.baseOffset(), batch.lastOffset(),\n                        batch.partitionLeaderEpoch(), batch.timestampType(), batch.maxTimestamp(),\n                        batch.isTransactional(), batch.isControlBatch());\n                filterResult.updateRetainedBatchMetadata(batch, 0, true);\n            }\n\n            // If we had to allocate a new buffer to fit the filtered buffer (see KAFKA-5316), return early to\n            // avoid the need for additional allocations.\n            ByteBuffer outputBuffer = bufferOutputStream.buffer();\n            if (outputBuffer != destinationBuffer) {\n                filterResult.outputBuffer = outputBuffer;\n                return filterResult;\n            }\n        }\n\n        return filterResult;\n    }\n\n    private static BatchFilterResult filterBatch(RecordBatch batch,\n                                                 BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier,\n                                                 FilterResult filterResult,\n                                                 RecordFilter filter) {\n        try (final CloseableIterator<Record> iterator = batch.streamingIterator(decompressionBufferSupplier)) {\n            long maxOffset = -1;\n            boolean containsTombstones = false;\n            // Convert records with old record versions\n            boolean writeOriginalBatch = batch.magic() >= RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE;\n            List<Record> retainedRecords = new ArrayList<>();\n            while (iterator.hasNext()) {\n                Record record = iterator.next();\n                filterResult.messagesRead += 1;\n\n                if (filter.shouldRetainRecord(batch, record)) {\n                    if (record.offset() > maxOffset)\n                        maxOffset = record.offset();\n\n                    retainedRecords.add(record);\n\n                    if (!record.hasValue()) {\n                        containsTombstones = true;\n                    }\n                } else {\n                    writeOriginalBatch = false;\n                }\n            }\n            return new BatchFilterResult(retainedRecords, writeOriginalBatch, containsTombstones, maxOffset);\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static class BatchFilterResult {\n        private final List<Record> retainedRecords;\n        private final boolean writeOriginalBatch;\n        private final boolean containsTombstones;\n        private final long maxOffset;\n        private BatchFilterResult(List<Record> retainedRecords,\n                                  final boolean writeOriginalBatch,\n                                  final boolean containsTombstones,\n                                  final long maxOffset) {\n            this.retainedRecords = retainedRecords;\n            this.writeOriginalBatch = writeOriginalBatch;\n            this.containsTombstones = containsTombstones;\n            this.maxOffset = maxOffset;\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static MemoryRecordsBuilder buildRetainedRecordsInto(RecordBatch originalBatch,\n                                                                 List<Record> retainedRecords,\n                                                                 ByteBufferOutputStream bufferOutputStream,\n                                                                 final long deleteHorizonMs) {\n        Compression compression = Compression.of(originalBatch.compressionType()).build();\n        // V0 has no timestamp type or timestamp, so we set the timestamp to CREATE_TIME and timestamp to NO_TIMESTAMP.\n        // Note that this differs from produce up-conversion where the timestamp type topic config is used and the log append\n        // time is generated if the config is LOG_APPEND_TIME. The reason for the different behavior is that there is\n        // no appropriate log append time we can generate at compaction time.\n        TimestampType timestampType = originalBatch.timestampType() == TimestampType.NO_TIMESTAMP_TYPE ?\n                TimestampType.CREATE_TIME : originalBatch.timestampType();\n        long logAppendTime = timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME ?\n                originalBatch.maxTimestamp() : RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        long baseOffset = originalBatch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2 ?\n                originalBatch.baseOffset() : retainedRecords.get(0).offset();\n\n        // Convert records with older record versions to the current one\n        MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = new MemoryRecordsBuilder(bufferOutputStream, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE,\n                compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime, originalBatch.producerId(),\n                originalBatch.producerEpoch(), originalBatch.baseSequence(), originalBatch.isTransactional(),\n                originalBatch.isControlBatch(), originalBatch.partitionLeaderEpoch(), bufferOutputStream.limit(), deleteHorizonMs);\n\n        for (Record record : retainedRecords)\n            builder.append(record);\n\n        if (originalBatch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2)\n            // we must preserve the last offset from the initial batch in order to ensure that the\n            // last sequence number from the batch remains even after compaction. Otherwise, the producer\n            // could incorrectly see an out of sequence error.\n            builder.overrideLastOffset(originalBatch.lastOffset());\n\n        return builder;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Get a read-only duplicate view of the {@link ByteBuffer} that backs this instance.\n     *\n     * <p>The returned buffer shares the underlying byte array with this instance \u2014 no data is\n     * copied. Its position is reset to 0 and its limit reflects the full size of the records\n     * data. Modifications to the returned buffer's position and limit do not affect this instance,\n     * but mutations to the underlying bytes (e.g. via in-place {@link MutableRecordBatch} methods)\n     * will be visible through both the returned buffer and this instance.\n     *\n     * @return a duplicate of the backing {@link ByteBuffer} starting at position 0\n     */\n    public ByteBuffer buffer() {\n        return buffer.duplicate();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Returns a zero-copy {@link MemoryRecords} view over a sub-range of this instance's backing\n     * buffer. The slice shares the underlying bytes; no data is copied.\n     *\n     * <p>If {@code size} exceeds the number of bytes available from {@code position} to the end\n     * of the buffer, the slice is silently clamped to the available bytes.\n     *\n     * @param position the start position (0-based, inclusive) within this instance's buffer\n     * @param size     the desired number of bytes in the slice\n     * @return a new {@link MemoryRecords} backed by the specified sub-range\n     * @throws IllegalArgumentException if {@code position} is negative, {@code position} exceeds\n     *         the buffer limit, or {@code size} is negative\n     */\n    @Override\n    public MemoryRecords slice(int position, int size) {\n        if (position < 0)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid position: \" + position + \" in read from \" + this);\n        if (position > buffer.limit())\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Slice from position \" + position + \" exceeds end position of \" + this);\n        if (size < 0)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid size: \" + size + \" in read from \" + this);\n\n        int availableBytes = Math.min(size, buffer.limit() - position);\n        // As of now, clients module support Java11 hence can't use ByteBuffer::slice(position, size) method.\n        // So we need to create a duplicate buffer and set the position and limit. Duplicate buffer\n        // is backed by original bytes hence not the content but only the relative position and limit\n        // are changed in the duplicate buffer. Once the position and limit are set, we can call the\n        // slice method to get the sliced buffer, which is a backed by the original buffer with the\n        // position reset to 0 and limit set to the size of the slice.\n        ByteBuffer slicedBuffer = buffer.duplicate();\n        slicedBuffer.position(position);\n        slicedBuffer.limit(position + availableBytes);\n        // Reset the position to 0 so that the sliced view has a relative position.\n        slicedBuffer = slicedBuffer.slice();\n\n        return readableRecords(slicedBuffer);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Returns an {@link Iterable} over the {@link MutableRecordBatch} objects contained in this\n     * instance. The iterable is backed by a lazy {@link #batchIterator()} and can be iterated\n     * multiple times; each call to {@link Iterable#iterator()} creates a new independent iterator\n     * over the same underlying buffer.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Performance note:</b> Batch-level metadata (offsets, timestamps, compression type) is\n     * read directly from the backing buffer without decompression. Record-level access requires\n     * explicit iteration into each batch.\n     *\n     * @return an {@link Iterable} of {@link MutableRecordBatch}; never {@code null}\n     */\n    @Override\n    public Iterable<MutableRecordBatch> batches() {\n        return batches;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public String toString() {\n        return \"MemoryRecords(size=\" + sizeInBytes() +\n                \", buffer=\" + buffer +\n                \")\";\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean equals(Object o) {\n        if (this == o)\n            return true;\n        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass())\n            return false;\n\n        MemoryRecords that = (MemoryRecords) o;\n\n        return buffer.equals(that.buffer);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int hashCode() {\n        return buffer.hashCode();\n    }\n\n    public abstract static class RecordFilter {\n        public final long currentTime;\n        public final long deleteRetentionMs;\n\n        public RecordFilter(final long currentTime, final long deleteRetentionMs) {\n            this.currentTime = currentTime;\n            this.deleteRetentionMs = deleteRetentionMs;\n        }\n\n BatchRetentionResult(final BatchRetention batchRetention,\n                                        final boolean containsMarkerForEmptyTxn) {\n                this.batchRetention = batchRetention;\n                this.containsMarkerForEmptyTxn = containsMarkerForEmptyTxn;\n            }\n        }\n\n        public enum BatchRetention {\n            DELETE, // Delete the batch without inspecting records\n            RETAIN_EMPTY, // Retain the batch even if it is empty\n            DELETE_EMPTY  // Delete the batch if it is empty\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Check whether the full retainedBatch.lastOffset(), numMessagesInBatch, bytesRetained);\n        }\n\n        private void updateRetainedBatchMetadata(long maxTimestamp, long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp, long maxOffset,\n                                                 int messagesRetained, int bytesRetained) {\n            validateBatchMetadata(maxTimestamp, shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp, maxOffset);\n            if (maxTimestamp > this.maxTimestamp) {\n                this.maxTimestamp = maxTimestamp;\n                this.shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp = shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp;\n            }\n            this.maxOffset = Math.max(maxOffset, this.maxOffset);\n            this.messagesRetained += messagesRetained;\n            this.bytesRetained += bytesRetained;\n        }\n\n        private void validateBatchMetadata(long maxTimestamp, long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp, long maxOffset) {\n            if (maxTimestamp != RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP && shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp < 0)\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"shallowOffset undefined for maximum timestamp \" + maxTimestamp);\n            if (maxOffset < 0)\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"maxOffset undefined\");\n        }\n\n        public ByteBuffer outputBuffer() {\n            return outputBuffer;\n        }\n\n        public int messagesRead() {\n            return messagesRead;\n        }\n\n        public int bytesRead() {\n            return bytesRead;\n        }\n\n        public int messagesRetained() {\n            return messagesRetained;\n        }\n\n        public int bytesRetained() {\n            return bytesRetained;\n        }\n\n        public long maxOffset() {\n            return maxOffset;\n        }\n\n        public long The\n     * buffer's current position is treated as the start of the first batch; the limit determines\n     * the total readable size.\n     *\n     * <p>No data is copied \u2014 the returned instance shares the underlying byte array with the\n     * supplied buffer.\n     *\n     * @param buffer the buffer containing encoded record batches; must not be {@code null}\n     * @return a {@link MemoryRecords} backed by {@code buffer}\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords readableRecords(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n        return new MemoryRecords(buffer);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} for constructing a new batch using the current magic\n     * version, the given compression and timestamp type, and starting at {@code baseOffset}.\n     *\n     * @param buffer        the buffer to write the encoded batch into; must not be {@code null}\n     * @param compression   the compression codec to apply to record data\n     * @param timestampType the timestamp type ({@link TimestampType#CREATE_TIME} or\n     *                      {@link TimestampType#LOG_APPEND_TIME})\n     * @param baseOffset    the base offset of the first record in the batch\n     * @return a new {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} ready to accept records\n     * @see MemoryRecordsBuilder\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset) {\n        return builder(buffer, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, compression, timestampType, baseOffset);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} for constructing a new batch using the current magic\n     * version, the given compression and timestamp type, starting at {@code baseOffset}, and\n     * capped at {@code maxSize} bytes.\n     *\n     * <p>When the timestamp type is {@link TimestampType#LOG_APPEND_TIME}, the log-append\n     * timestamp is set to the current wall-clock time at the moment this method is called.\n     *\n     * @param buffer        the buffer to write the encoded batch into; must not be {@code null}\n     * @param compression   the compression codec to apply to record data\n     * @param timestampType the timestamp type\n     * @param baseOffset    the base offset of the first record in the batch\n     * @param maxSize       maximum number of bytes the builder may write into {@code buffer}\n     * @return a new {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} ready to accept records\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                                               int maxSize) {\n        long logAppendTime = RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        if (timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME)\n            logAppendTime = System.currentTimeMillis();\n\n        return new MemoryRecordsBuilder(buffer, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, compression, timestampType, baseOffset,\n            logAppendTime, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_ID, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH, RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE,\n            false, false, RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH, maxSize);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} with the specified magic version, compression,\n     * timestamp type, and explicit log-append time. No idempotent or transactional producer\n     * metadata is set.\n     *\n     * @param buffer        the buffer to write the encoded batch into; must not be {@code null}\n     * @param magic         the record format magic byte\n     * @param compression   the compression codec to apply to record data\n     * @param timestampType the timestamp type\n     * @param baseOffset    the base offset of the first record in the batch\n     * @param logAppendTime the log-append timestamp to embed in the batch header;\n     *                      use {@link RecordBatch#NO_TIMESTAMP} if not applicable\n     * @return a new {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} ready to accept records\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               byte magic,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                                               long logAppendTime) {\n        return builder(buffer, magic, compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_ID, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH, RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE, false,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} with the specified magic version, compression, and\n     * timestamp type. The log-append timestamp is set automatically if the timestamp type is\n     * {@link TimestampType#LOG_APPEND_TIME}. No idempotent or transactional producer metadata is\n     * set.\n     *\n     * @param buffer        the buffer to write the encoded batch into; must not be {@code null}\n     * @param magic         the record format magic byte\n     * @param compression   the compression codec to apply to record data\n     * @param timestampType the timestamp type\n     * @param baseOffset    the base offset of the first record in the batch\n     * @return a new {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} ready to accept records\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               byte magic,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset) {\n        long logAppendTime = RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        if (timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME)\n            logAppendTime = System.currentTimeMillis();\n        return builder(buffer, magic, compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_ID, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH, RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE, false,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} with the specified magic version, compression,\n     * timestamp type, log-append time, and partition leader epoch. No idempotent or transactional\n     * producer metadata is set.\n     *\n     * @param buffer               the buffer to write the encoded batch into; must not be {@code null}\n     * @param magic                the record format magic byte\n     * @param compression          the compression codec to apply to record data\n     * @param timestampType        the timestamp type\n     * @param baseOffset           the base offset of the first record in the batch\n     * @param logAppendTime        the log-append timestamp;\n     *                             use {@link RecordBatch#NO_TIMESTAMP} if not applicable\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch the partition leader epoch to embed in the batch header\n     * @return a new {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} ready to accept records\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               byte magic,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                                               long logAppendTime,\n                                               int partitionLeaderEpoch) {\n        return builder(buffer, magic, compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_ID, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH, RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE, false, partitionLeaderEpoch);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} for building a transactional or idempotent batch\n     * using the current magic version and {@link TimestampType#CREATE_TIME}. The producer\n     * identity ({@code producerId}, {@code producerEpoch}, {@code baseSequence}) and the\n     * transactional flag are embedded in the batch header.\n     *\n     * @param buffer          the buffer to write the encoded batch into; must not be {@code null}\n     * @param compression     the compression codec to apply to record data\n     * @param baseOffset      the base offset of the first record in the batch\n     * @param producerId      the idempotent/transactional producer id\n     * @param producerEpoch   the producer epoch\n     * @param baseSequence    the base sequence number for duplicate detection\n     * @param isTransactional {@code true} if the batch is part of an ongoing transaction\n     * @return a new {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} ready to accept records\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                                               long producerId,\n                                               short producerEpoch,\n                                               int baseSequence,\n                                               boolean isTransactional) {\n        return builder(buffer, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, compression, TimestampType.CREATE_TIME, baseOffset,\n                RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP, producerId, producerEpoch, baseSequence, isTransactional,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} with the given magic version, compression, timestamp\n     * type, log-append time, and full idempotent producer metadata. The batch is non-transactional\n     * and uses {@link RecordBatch#NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH}.\n     *\n     * @param buffer        the buffer to write the encoded batch into; must not be {@code null}\n     * @param magic         the record format magic byte\n     * @param compression   the compression codec to apply to record data\n     * @param timestampType the timestamp type\n     * @param baseOffset    the base offset of the first record in the batch\n     * @param logAppendTime the log-append timestamp;\n     *                      use {@link RecordBatch#NO_TIMESTAMP} if not applicable\n     * @param producerId    the idempotent/transactional producer id\n     * @param producerEpoch the producer epoch\n     * @param baseSequence  the base sequence number for duplicate detection\n     * @return a new {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} ready to accept records\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               byte magic,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                                               long logAppendTime,\n                                               long producerId,\n                                               short producerEpoch,\n                                               int baseSequence) {\n        return builder(buffer, magic, compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime,\n                producerId, producerEpoch, baseSequence, false, RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} with full control over magic version, compression,\n     * timestamp type, log-append time, producer identity, transactional flag, and partition leader\n     * epoch. The control-batch flag is set to {@code false}.\n     *\n     * @param buffer               the buffer to write the encoded batch into; must not be {@code null}\n     * @param magic                the the producer epoch, or {@link RecordBatch#NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH}\n     * @param baseSequence         the base sequence number, or {@link RecordBatch#NO_SEQUENCE}\n     * @param isTransactional      {@code true} if the batch belongs to a transaction\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch the partition leader epoch at the time of writing\n     * @return a new {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} ready to accept Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                                               long logAppendTime,\n                                               long producerId,\n                                               short producerEpoch,\n                                               int baseSequence,\n                                               boolean isTransactional,\n                                               int partitionLeaderEpoch) {\n        return builder(buffer, magic, compression, timestampType, baseOffset,\n                logAppendTime, producerId, producerEpoch, baseSequence, isTransactional, false, partitionLeaderEpoch);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} with full control over all batch header fields,\n     * including the control-batch flag.\n     *\n     * @param buffer               the buffer to write the encoded batch into; must not be {@code null}\n     * @param magic                the record format magic byte\n     * @param compression          the compression codec to apply to record data\n     * @param timestampType        the timestamp type\n     * @param baseOffset           the base offset of the first record in the batch\n     * @param logAppendTime        the log-append timestamp;\n     *                             use {@link RecordBatch#NO_TIMESTAMP} if not applicable\n     * @param producerId           the idempotent/transactional producer id, or\n     *                             {@link RecordBatch#NO_PRODUCER_ID}\n     * @param producerEpoch        the producer epoch, or {@link RecordBatch#NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH}\n     * @param baseSequence         the base Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                                               long logAppendTime,\n                                               long producerId,\n                                               short producerEpoch,\n                                               int baseSequence,\n                                               boolean isTransactional,\n                                               boolean isControlBatch,\n                                               int partitionLeaderEpoch) {\n        return new MemoryRecordsBuilder(buffer, magic, compression, timestampType, baseOffset,\n                logAppendTime, producerId, producerEpoch, baseSequence, isTransactional, isControlBatch, partitionLeaderEpoch,\n                buffer.remaining());\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Builds a {@link MemoryRecords} containing the given The timestamp type is {@link TimestampType#CREATE_TIME}.\n     *\n     * @param initialOffset        the base offset to assign to the first record\n     * @param compression          the compression codec to apply\n     * @param producerId           the transactional producer id\n     * @param producerEpoch        the producer epoch\n     * @param baseSequence         the base sequence number\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch the partition leader epoch\n     * @param records              the records to include; varargs\n     * @return an immutable {@link MemoryRecords} containing the serialised transactional batch\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withTransactionalRecords(long initialOffset, Compression compression, long producerId,\n                                                         short producerEpoch, int baseSequence, int partitionLeaderEpoch,\n                                                         SimpleRecord... records) {\n        return withTransactionalRecords(RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, initialOffset, compression,\n                producerId, producerEpoch, baseSequence, partitionLeaderEpoch, records);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Builds a {@link MemoryRecords} containing the given {@link SimpleRecord} objects using the\n     * specified magic version, initial offset, compression, and timestamp type. No idempotent or\n     * transactional metadata is embedded.\n     *\n     * @param magic         the record format magic byte\n     * @param initialOffset the base offset to assign to the first record\n     * @param compression   the compression codec to apply\n     * @param timestampType the timestamp type\n     * @param records       the records to include; varargs\n     * @return an immutable {@link MemoryRecords} containing the serialised batch\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withRecords(byte magic, long initialOffset, Compression compression,\n                                            TimestampType timestampType, SimpleRecord... records) {\n        return withRecords(magic, initialOffset, compression, timestampType, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_ID,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH, RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE, RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH,\n                false, records);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Builds a {@link MemoryRecords} containing the given {@link SimpleRecord} objects with full\n     * control over all batch header fields. This is the most general {@code withRecords} overload;\n     * all other overloads delegate to this method.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Performance note:</b> The method estimates the required buffer size upfront based on\n     * {@link AbstractRecords#estimateSizeInBytes} and uses a resizable\n     * {@link ByteBufferOutputStream} to handle cases where the estimate is too small. Only a\n     * single batch is created per call.\n     *\n     * @param magic                the record format magic byte\n     * @param initialOffset        the base offset to assign to the first record\n     * @param compression          the compression codec to apply\n     * @param timestampType        the timestamp type\n     * @param producerId           the idempotent/transactional producer id, or\n     *                             {@link RecordBatch#NO_PRODUCER_ID}\n     * @param producerEpoch        the producer epoch, or {@link RecordBatch#NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH}\n     * @param baseSequence         the base sequence number, or {@link RecordBatch#NO_SEQUENCE}\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch the partition leader epoch\n     * @param isTransactional      {@code true} if the batch belongs to a transaction\n     * @param records              the records to include; varargs\n     * @return an immutable {@link MemoryRecords} containing the serialised batch, or\n     *         {@link #EMPTY} if {@code records} is empty\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withRecords(byte magic, long initialOffset, Compression compression,\n                                            TimestampType timestampType, long producerId, short producerEpoch,\n                                            int baseSequence, int partitionLeaderEpoch, boolean isTransactional,\n                                            SimpleRecord... records) {\n        if (records.length == 0)\n            return MemoryRecords.EMPTY;\n        int sizeEstimate = AbstractRecords.estimateSizeInBytes(magic, compression.type(), Arrays.asList(records));\n        ByteBufferOutputStream bufferStream = new ByteBufferOutputStream(sizeEstimate);\n        long logAppendTime = RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        if (timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME)\n            logAppendTime = System.currentTimeMillis();\n        try (final MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = new MemoryRecordsBuilder(bufferStream, magic, compression, timestampType,\n                initialOffset, logAppendTime, producerId, producerEpoch, baseSequence, isTransactional, false,\n                partitionLeaderEpoch, sizeEstimate)) {\n            for (SimpleRecord record : records)\n                builder.append(record);\n            return builder.build();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Builds a {@link MemoryRecords} containing a single end-of-transaction control batch for the\n     * given producer, using offset 0 and the current wall-clock time as the timestamp.\n     *\n     * @param producerId    the {@link MemoryRecords} containing the end-transaction control batch\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withEndTransactionMarker(long producerId, short producerEpoch, EndTransactionMarker marker) {\n        return withEndTransactionMarker(0L, System.currentTimeMillis(), RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH,\n                producerId, producerEpoch, marker);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Builds
